class[EllipticCurve](https://hackage.haskell.org/package/cryptonite-0.30/docs/Crypto-ECC.html#t:EllipticCurve "Crypto.ECC") curve =>[EllipticCurveDH](https://hackage.haskell.org/package/cryptonite-0.30/docs/Crypto-ECC.html) curve where[Source](https://hackage.haskell.org/package/cryptonite-0.30/docs/src/Crypto.ECC.html#EllipticCurveDH)[#](https://hackage.haskell.org/package/cryptonite-0.30/docs/Crypto-ECC.html#t:EllipticCurveDH)

Minimal complete definition

[ecdh](https://hackage.haskell.org/package/cryptonite-0.30/docs/Crypto-ECC.html#v:ecdh "Crypto.ECC")

Methods

[ecdhRaw](https://hackage.haskell.org/package/cryptonite-0.30/docs/Crypto-ECC.html) :: proxy curve ->[Scalar](https://hackage.haskell.org/package/cryptonite-0.30/docs/Crypto-ECC.html#t:Scalar "Crypto.ECC") curve ->[Point](https://hackage.haskell.org/package/cryptonite-0.30/docs/Crypto-ECC.html#t:Point "Crypto.ECC") curve ->[SharedSecret](https://hackage.haskell.org/package/cryptonite-0.30/docs/Crypto-ECC.html#t:SharedSecret "Crypto.ECC")[Source](https://hackage.haskell.org/package/cryptonite-0.30/docs/src/Crypto.ECC.html#ecdhRaw)[#](https://hackage.haskell.org/package/cryptonite-0.30/docs/Crypto-ECC.html#v:ecdhRaw)

Generate a Diffie hellman secret value.

This is generally just the .x coordinate of the resulting point, that is not hashed.

use `pointSmul` to keep the result in Point format.

_WARNING:_ Curve implementations may return a special value or an exception when the public point lies in a subgroup of small order. This function is adequate when the scalar is in expected range and contributory behaviour is not needed. Otherwise use `ecdh`.

[ecdh](https://hackage.haskell.org/package/cryptonite-0.30/docs/Crypto-ECC.html) :: proxy curve ->[Scalar](https://hackage.haskell.org/package/cryptonite-0.30/docs/Crypto-ECC.html#t:Scalar "Crypto.ECC") curve ->[Point](https://hackage.haskell.org/package/cryptonite-0.30/docs/Crypto-ECC.html#t:Point "Crypto.ECC") curve ->[CryptoFailable](https://hackage.haskell.org/package/cryptonite-0.30/docs/Crypto-Error.html#t:CryptoFailable "Crypto.Error")[SharedSecret](https://hackage.haskell.org/package/cryptonite-0.30/docs/Crypto-ECC.html#t:SharedSecret "Crypto.ECC")[Source](https://hackage.haskell.org/package/cryptonite-0.30/docs/src/Crypto.ECC.html#ecdh)[#](https://hackage.haskell.org/package/cryptonite-0.30/docs/Crypto-ECC.html#v:ecdh)

Generate a Diffie hellman secret value and verify that the result is not the point at infinity.

This additional test avoids risks existing with function `ecdhRaw`. Implementations always return a `CryptoError` instead of a special value or an exception.
